insert into WoodPallet (CreatedDate,LocationID,PalletType,RefPalletOutside,Archive)
select distinct CAST(GETDATE() AS DATE),2,ItemTypeID,Bulto,0 from TempPallet
GO

INSERT INTO WoodPalletItem (WoodPalletID,StockItemID,Width,Length,Quantity,QuantityUsed,OutstandingQty,Description,StockCode,Thickness)
select distinct
WP.WoodPalletID,
SI.StockItemID,
TP.Ancho,
TP.Largo,
TP.Cantidad,
0,
TP.Cantidad,
SI.Description,
SI.StockCode,
SI.Thickness

from TempPallet TP
left join StockItem SI on SI.Species= TP.SpeciesID and SI.Thickness=tp.Grosor and SI.ItemType = TP.ItemTypeID
left join WoodPallet WP on WP.RefPalletOutside=TP.Bulto

go

drop table TempPallet
go
